Script_4\_AdditionalAnalyses
================
Linda Dieckmann
November 2022

In this script we test if maximum glycyrrhizin during pregnancy shows
influence on gene expression and we test differential expression for
different pregnancy stages

# load packages

``` r
library(here)
```

# Pre-Processing for Differential Expression Analysis

## load input for this part

### expression counts

``` r
load(here("02_Data/RNA/", "all_final_counts_for_analyses.Rdata"))
```

``` r
load(here("02_Data/RNA/", "annotation_genes_placenta_rna.Rdata"))
load(here("02_Data/RNA/", "annotation_genes_cvs_rna.Rdata"))
```

### phenotypes

``` r
load(here("02_Data/pheno/", "all_phenos_rna.Rdata"))
```

## subset data

*relevant covariates*

``` r
covariates_rna_placenta <- c("SV1", "Gestational_Age_Weeks", "Child_Sex", "Maternal_Body_Mass_Index_in_Early_Pregnancy", "Delivery_mode_3l")
covariates_rna_cvs <- c("SV1", "gestage_at_CVS_weeks", "Child_Sex", "Maternal_Body_Mass_Index_in_Early_Pregnancy", "Delivery_mode_3l")
```

*subset data for relevant variables*

``` r
p_rna_placenta_max_preg <- pheno_rna_placenta_maxpreg[,c("IDfamily", covariates_rna_placenta, "gly_trim_mg_max_over_pregnancy_winsz")]
```

``` r
p_rna_placenta_stage_I <- pheno_rna_placenta_stages_I[,c("IDfamily", covariates_rna_placenta, "gly_trim_mg_q_pregstageMean_winsz")]
p_rna_placenta_stage_II <- pheno_rna_placenta_stages_II[,c("IDfamily", covariates_rna_placenta, "gly_trim_mg_q_pregstageMean_winsz")]
p_rna_placenta_stage_III <- pheno_rna_placenta_stages_III[,c("IDfamily", covariates_rna_placenta, "gly_trim_mg_q_pregstageMean_winsz")]
```

## make DGE object

### We create the DGE lists

``` r
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg <- DGEList(counts_placenta_filtered_final)
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I <- DGEList(counts_placenta_filtered_final_s1)
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II <- DGEList(counts_placenta_filtered_final_s2)
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III <- DGEList(counts_placenta_filtered_final_s3)
```

### organizing sample information

``` r
p_rna_placenta_max_preg <- order_rows_same(df_to_order = p_rna_placenta_max_preg, df_template_vector = colnames(DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg))
p_rna_placenta_stage_I <- order_rows_same(df_to_order = p_rna_placenta_stage_I, df_template_vector = colnames(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I))
p_rna_placenta_stage_II <- order_rows_same(df_to_order = p_rna_placenta_stage_II, df_template_vector = colnames(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II))
p_rna_placenta_stage_III <- order_rows_same(df_to_order = p_rna_placenta_stage_III, df_template_vector = colnames(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III))
```

``` r
identical(colnames(DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg), p_rna_placenta_max_preg$IDfamily)
```

### add the phenotypes to DGE object

``` r
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples$glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz <- p_rna_placenta_max_preg$gly_trim_mg_max_over_pregnancy_winsz
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples$sv1 <- p_rna_placenta_max_preg$SV1
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples$gestational_age <- p_rna_placenta_max_preg$Gestational_Age_Weeks
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples$child_sex <- p_rna_placenta_max_preg$Child_Sex
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples$bmi <- p_rna_placenta_max_preg$Maternal_Body_Mass_Index_in_Early_Pregnancy
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples$delivery_mode <- p_rna_placenta_max_preg$Delivery_mode_3l
```

``` r
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I$samples$glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz <- p_rna_placenta_stage_I$gly_trim_mg_q_pregstageMean_winsz

DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I$samples$child_sex <- p_rna_placenta_stage_I$Child_Sex

```

``` r
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II$samples$glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz <- p_rna_placenta_stage_II$gly_trim_mg_q_pregstageMean_winsz
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II$samples$sv1 <- p_rna_placenta_stage_II$SV1
```

``` r
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III$samples$glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz <- p_rna_placenta_stage_III$gly_trim_mg_q_pregstageMean_winsz
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III$samples$sv1 <- p_rna_placenta_stage_III$SV1
```

## Normalization

``` r
DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg <- calcNormFactors(DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg, method = "TMM")
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I <- calcNormFactors(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I, method = "TMM")
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II <- calcNormFactors(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II, method = "TMM")
DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III <- calcNormFactors(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III, method = "TMM")
```

# Differential Expresssion

``` r
load(here("02_Data/pre_processed/", "DGE_rna_add.Rdata"))
```

## Placenta maximum consumption over pregnancy

### model matrix

``` r
main_predictor_rna_placenta <- "glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz"

x_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples[[main_predictor_rna_placenta]]
```

``` r
cov1_rna_placenta <- "sv1"
cov2_rna_placenta <- c("gestational_age", "child_sex", "bmi", "delivery_mode")

x1_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples[[cov1_rna_placenta]]
x2_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$samples[cov2_rna_placenta]
```

``` r
# basic model
model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta)

# covariate adjusted model
model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta + x2_rna_placenta$gestational_age + x2_rna_placenta$child_sex + x2_rna_placenta$bmi + x2_rna_placenta$delivery_mode)
```

### model

``` r
# basic model
voom_basic_rna_placenta <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_basic_rna_placenta <- lmFit(voom_basic_rna_placenta, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta)
fit_basic_rna_placenta <- contrasts.fit(fit_basic_rna_placenta, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption (2 because we have intercept)
efit_basic_rna_placenta <- eBayes(fit_basic_rna_placenta, robust = T)

top.table_basic_rna_placenta <- topTable(efit_basic_rna_placenta, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_basic_rna_placenta, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/max/basic_placenta/", "top.table_basic_rna_placenta.xlsx"))
```

``` r
# covariate adjusted model
voom_adjusted_rna_placenta <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta <- lmFit(voom_adjusted_rna_placenta, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta <- contrasts.fit(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption
efit_adjusted_rna_placenta <- eBayes(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta, robust = T)
top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta <- topTable(efit_adjusted_rna_placenta, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/max/adjusted_placenta/", "top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta.xlsx"))
```

``` r
glMDPlot(efit_adjusted_rna_placenta, coef=1, status=dt_adjusted_rna_placenta[,1], main=colnames(efit_adjusted_rna_placenta)[1], counts=DGE_placenta_rna_max_preg$counts, groups= x_rna_placenta, launch = F, path = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/max/adjusted_placenta/"), html = "MD-Plot_adjusted_placenta")
```

## Placenta consumption first pregnancy stage

``` r
cat("We have", nrow(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I$samples), "samples for this stage")
```

    ## We have 306 samples for this stage

### model matrix

``` r
main_predictor_rna_placenta <- "glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz"

x_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I$samples[[main_predictor_rna_placenta]]
```

``` r
cov1_rna_placenta <- "sv1"
cov2_rna_placenta <- c("gestational_age", "child_sex", "bmi", "delivery_mode")

x1_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I$samples[[cov1_rna_placenta]]
x2_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I$samples[cov2_rna_placenta]
```

``` r
# basic model
model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta)

# covariate adjusted model
model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta + x2_rna_placenta$gestational_age + x2_rna_placenta$child_sex + x2_rna_placenta$bmi + x2_rna_placenta$delivery_mode)
```

### model

``` r
# basic model
voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I <- lmFit(voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta)
fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I <- contrasts.fit(fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption (2 because we have intercept)
efit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I <- eBayes(fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I, robust = T)

top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I <- topTable(efit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_I/basic_placenta/", "top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I.xlsx"))
```

``` r
# covariate adjusted model
voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_I, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I <- lmFit(voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I <- contrasts.fit(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption
efit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I <- eBayes(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I, robust = T)
top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I <- topTable(efit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_I/adjusted_placenta/", "top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I.xlsx"))
```

``` r
# basic
gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I <- top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I[top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I$hgnc_symbol %in% "HSD11B2", ]
```

``` r
# adjusted
gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I <- top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I[top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I$hgnc_symbol %in% "HSD11B2", ]

write.table(gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_I/adjusted_placenta/", "gene_of_interest_statistic_stage_I.txt"), quote = F)
```

plot gene

``` r
# extract info
rna_variables_basic_placenta_stage_I <- voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I$targets[,c(main_predictor_rna_placenta, cov1_rna_placenta)]
expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I <- voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I$E
rna_variables_basic_placenta_stage_I$HSD11B2_expression <- expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I[rownames(expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I) %in% gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I[gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_I$hgnc_symbol == "HSD11B2", "ensembl_gene_id"], ]

rna_variables_adjusted_placenta_stage_I <- voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I$targets[,c(main_predictor_rna_placenta, cov1_rna_placenta, cov2_rna_placenta)]
expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I <- voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I$E
rna_variables_adjusted_placenta_stage_I$HSD11B2_expression <- expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I[rownames(expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I) %in% gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I[gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_I$hgnc_symbol == "HSD11B2", "ensembl_gene_id"], ]
```

## Placenta consumption second pregnancy stage

``` r
cat("We have", nrow(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II$samples), "samples for this stage")
```

    ## We have 387 samples for this stage

### model matrix

``` r
main_predictor_rna_placenta <- "glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz"

x_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II$samples[[main_predictor_rna_placenta]]
```

``` r
cov1_rna_placenta <- "sv1"
cov2_rna_placenta <- c("gestational_age", "child_sex", "bmi", "delivery_mode")

x1_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II$samples[[cov1_rna_placenta]]
x2_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II$samples[cov2_rna_placenta]
```

``` r
# basic model
model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta)

# covariate adjusted model
model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta + x2_rna_placenta$gestational_age + x2_rna_placenta$child_sex + x2_rna_placenta$bmi + x2_rna_placenta$delivery_mode)
```

### model

``` r
# basic model
voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II <- lmFit(voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta)
fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II <- contrasts.fit(fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption (2 because we have intercept)
efit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II <- eBayes(fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II, robust = T)

top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II <- topTable(efit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_II/basic_placenta/", "top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II.xlsx"))
```

``` r
# covariate adjusted model
voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_II, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II <- lmFit(voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II <- contrasts.fit(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption
efit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II <- eBayes(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II, robust = T)
top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II <- topTable(efit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_II/adjusted_placenta/", "top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II.xlsx"))
```

``` r
# basic
gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II <- top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II[top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II$hgnc_symbol %in% "HSD11B2", ]
```

``` r
# adjusted
```

plot gene

``` r
# extract info
rna_variables_basic_placenta_stage_II <- voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II$targets[,c(main_predictor_rna_placenta, cov1_rna_placenta)]
expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II <- voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II$E
rna_variables_basic_placenta_stage_II$HSD11B2_expression <- expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II[rownames(expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II) %in% gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II[gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_II$hgnc_symbol == "HSD11B2", "ensembl_gene_id"], ]

rna_variables_adjusted_placenta_stage_II <- voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II$targets[,c(main_predictor_rna_placenta, cov1_rna_placenta, cov2_rna_placenta)]
expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II <- voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II$E
rna_variables_adjusted_placenta_stage_II$HSD11B2_expression <- expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II[rownames(expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II) %in% gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II[gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_II$hgnc_symbol == "HSD11B2", "ensembl_gene_id"], ]
```

## Placenta consumption third pregnancy stage

``` r
cat("We have", nrow(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III$samples), "samples for this stage")
```

    ## We have 397 samples for this stage

### model matrix

``` r
main_predictor_rna_placenta <- "glycyrrhizin_mg_winsz"

x_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III$samples[[main_predictor_rna_placenta]]
```

``` r
cov1_rna_placenta <- "sv1"
cov2_rna_placenta <- c("gestational_age", "child_sex", "bmi", "delivery_mode")

x1_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III$samples[[cov1_rna_placenta]]
x2_rna_placenta <- DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III$samples[cov2_rna_placenta]
```

``` r
# basic model
model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta)

# covariate adjusted model
model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta <- model.matrix(~ x_rna_placenta + x1_rna_placenta + x2_rna_placenta$gestational_age + x2_rna_placenta$child_sex + x2_rna_placenta$bmi + x2_rna_placenta$delivery_mode)
```

### model

``` r
# basic model
voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III <- lmFit(voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III, model_matrix_basic_rna_placenta)
fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III <- contrasts.fit(fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption (2 because we have intercept)
efit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III <- eBayes(fit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III, robust = T)

top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III <- topTable(efit_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_III/basic_placenta/", "top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III.xlsx"))
```

``` r
# covariate adjusted model
voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III <- voom(DGE_placenta_rna_stage_III, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta, plot = F)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III <- lmFit(voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III, model_matrix_adjusted_rna_placenta)
fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III <- contrasts.fit(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III, coef = 2) # test second coefficient, here glycyrrhizin consumption
efit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III <- eBayes(fit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III, robust = T)
top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III <- topTable(efit_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III, sort.by = "P", n = Inf)
```

``` r
write.xlsx(top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_III/adjusted_placenta/", "top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III.xlsx"))
```

``` r
# basic
```


### gene of interest

*HSD11B2*

extract statistics

``` r
# basic
gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III <- top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III[top.table_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III$hgnc_symbol %in% "HSD11B2", ]

write.table(gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_III/basic_placenta/", "gene_of_interest_statistic.txt"), quote = F)
```

``` r
# adjusted
gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III <- top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III[top.table_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III$hgnc_symbol %in% "HSD11B2", ]

write.table(gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III, file = here("Analyses/Results/differential_expression/additional/stage_III/adjusted_placenta/", "gene_of_interest_statistic_stage_III.txt"), quote = F)
```

plot gene

``` r
# extract info
rna_variables_basic_placenta_stage_III <- voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III$targets[,c(main_predictor_rna_placenta, cov1_rna_placenta)]
expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III <- voom_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III$E
rna_variables_basic_placenta_stage_III$HSD11B2_expression <- expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III[rownames(expression_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III) %in% gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III[gene_interest_basic_rna_placenta_stage_III$hgnc_symbol == "HSD11B2", "ensembl_gene_id"], ]

rna_variables_adjusted_placenta_stage_III <- voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III$targets[,c(main_predictor_rna_placenta, cov1_rna_placenta, cov2_rna_placenta)]
expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III <- voom_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III$E
rna_variables_adjusted_placenta_stage_III$HSD11B2_expression <- expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III[rownames(expression_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III) %in% gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III[gene_interest_adjusted_rna_placenta_stage_III$hgnc_symbol == "HSD11B2", "ensembl_gene_id"], ]
```

``` r
HSD11B2_expression_plot_placenta_cor_stage_III <- plot_gene_scatter(rna_variables_adjusted_placenta_stage_III, xtitle = "glycyrrhizin consumption (mg, winsorized) during first pregnancy stage", ytitle = "HSD11B2 expression (transformed counts)", maintitle = "Placenta Tissue first pregnancy stage")
HSD11B2_expression_plot_placenta_cor_stage_III
```
